| 0:03:39| fatalities on city-controlled roads by 2040.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=219)|

| 2:36:46| Council members, you all are familiar with the origins of the Behavioral Health Urgent Care Center, BHUC,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9406)|
| 2:36:52| which opened its doors in 2018.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9412)|
| 2:36:55| The BHUC is designed to divert adults from jail and the criminal justice system who could be better served| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9415)|
| 2:37:00| with connection to mental or substance abuse services.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9420)|
| 2:37:04| So every year, hundreds are diverted from incarceration.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9424)|
| 2:37:07| I also want to take a moment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9427)|
| 2:37:09| First of all, thank you to the McNabb Center for partnering with us on this and being so effective.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9429)|
| 2:37:14| I also want to take a moment to clarify the difference between the BHUC,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9434)|
| 2:37:17| which has been in place since 2018 and is on your agenda right now,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9437)|
| 2:37:21| and the MPATH unit that is being constructed at the St. Mary's site.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9441)|
| 2:37:25| MPATH stands for Emergency Psychiatric Assessment Treatment and Healing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9445)|
| 2:37:31| That facility will be designed to divert persons who have a mental illness,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9451)|
| 2:37:36| not necessarily from incarceration but from local emergency rooms,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9456)|
| 2:37:40| to a place that is designed to provide immediate psychiatric care and services with the goal of stabilization.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9460)|
| 2:37:46| So thank you for your support of both facilities that are critical in helping some of the most vulnerable in our city.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9466)|
| 2:37:53| Vice Mayor Roberto.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230822?start=9473)|
